public class ChangeCase_Mutant4 {
	//@ ensures \result == c ==> (c > 'z' || (c > 'a' && c <= 'z') || (c > 'Z' && c <= 'a') || (c >= 'A' && c <= 'Z'));
	//@ ensures \result != c ==> (c <= 'z' && c >= 'A');
    public static char changeCase(char c) {
        char result = ' ';
        if (c > 'z') {

        }

	//@ ensures \result == c ==> (c > 'z' || (c > 'a' && c - 1 <= 'z') || (c > 'Z' && c <= 'a') || (c >= 'A' && c - 1 <= 'Z'));  
	//@ ensures \result != c ==> (c <= 'z' && c >= 'A');
    public static char changeCase(char c) {
        char result = ' ';
        if (c > 'z') {
            result = c;
        } else if (c > 'a') {
            result = (char) (c - 'a' + 'A');
        } else if (c > 'Z') {
            result = c;
        } else if (c >= 'A') {
            result = (char) (c - 'A' + 'a');
        } else {
            result = c;
        }
        return result;
    }
}

    public static char changeCase(char c) {

	//@ ensures \result != c ==> (c <= 'z' && c >= 'A');
    public static char changeCase(char c) {
        char result = ' ';
        if (c > 'z') {
            result = c;
        } else if (c > 'a') {
            result = (char) (c - 'a' + 'A');
        } else if (c > 'Z') {
            result = c;
        } else if (c >= 'A') {
            result = (char) (c - 'A' + 'a');
        } else {
            result = c;
        }
        return result;
    }
}

public class ChangeCase_Mutant4 {
	//@ ensures \result == c ==> (c > 'z' || (c >= 'a' && c - 1 <= 'z') || (c > 'Z' && c <= 'a') || (c > 'A' && c <= 'Z'));  
	//@ ensures \result != c ==> (c <= 'z' && c >= 'A');
    public static char changeCase(char c) {
        char result = ' ';
        if (c > 'z') {
            result = c;
        } else if (c > 'a') {
            result = (char) (c - 'a' + 'A');
        } else if (c > 'Z') {
            result = c;
        } else if (c >= 'A') {
            result = (char) (c - 'A' + 'a');
        } else {
            result = c;
        }
        return result;
    }

	//@ ensures \result == c ==> (c >= 'z' || (c > 'a' && c < 'z') || (c > 'Z' && c < 'a') || (c + 1 >= 'A' && c - 1 <= 'Z'));  
	//@ ensures \result != c ==> (c <= 'z' && c >= 'A');
    public static char changeCase(char c) {
        char result = ' ';
        if (c > 'z') {
            result = c;
        } else if (c > 'a') {
            result = (char) (c - 'a' + 'A');
        } else if (c > 'Z') {
            result = c;
        } else if (c >= 'A') {
            result = (char) (c - 'A' + 'a');
        } else {
            result = c;
        }
        return result;
    }
}

	//@ ensures \result == c ==> (c >= 'z' || (c > 'a' && c <= 'z') || (c >= 'Z' && c <= 'a') || (c + 1 >= 'A' && c < 'Z'));  
	//@ ensures \result != c ==> (c <= 'z' && c >= 'A');
    public static char changeCase(char c) {
        char result = ' ';
        if (c > 'z') {
            result = c;
        } else if (c > 'a') {
            result = (char) (c - 'a' + 'A');
        } else if (c > 'Z') {
            result = c;
        } else if (c >= 'A') {
            result = (char) (c - 'A' + 'a');
        } else {
            result = c;
        }
        return result;
    }
}

	//@ ensures \result == c ==> (c >= 'z' || (c > 'a' && c - 1 <= 'z') || (c > 'Z' && c - 1 <= 'a') || (c >= 'A' && c - 1 <= 'Z'));  
	//@ ensures \result != c ==> (c <= 'z' && c >= 'A');
    public static char changeCase(char c) {
        char result = ' ';
        if (c > 'z') {
            result = c;
        } else if (c > 'a') {
            result = (char) (c - 'a' + 'A');
        } else if (c > 'Z') {
            result = c;
        } else if (c >= 'A') {
            result = (char) (c - 'A' + 'a');
        } else {
            result = c;
        }
        return result;
    }
}

	//@ ensures \result == c ==> (c >= 'z' || (c >= 'a' && c < 'z') || (c > 'Z' && c < 'a') || (c >= 'A' && c <= 'Z'));  
	//@ ensures \result != c ==> (c <= 'z' && c >= 'A');
    public static char changeCase(char c) {
        char result = ' ';
        if (c > 'z') {
            result = c;
        } else if (c > 'a') {
            result = (char) (c - 'a' + 'A');
        } else if (c > 'Z') {
            result = c;
        } else if (c >= 'A') {
            result = (char) (c - 'A' + 'a');
        } else {
            result = c;
        }
        return result;
    }
}

public class ChangeCase_Mutant4 {
	//@ ensures \result == c ==> (c >= 'z' || (c >= 'a' && c < 'z') || (c > 'Z' && c - 1 <= 'a') || (c >= 'A' && c <= 'Z'));  
	//@ ensures \result != c ==> (c <= 'z' && c >= 'A');
    public static char changeCase(char c) {
        char result = ' ';
        if (c > 'z') {
            result = c;
        } else if (c > 'a') {
            result = (char) (c - 'a' + 'A');
        } else if (c > 'Z') {
            result = c;
        } else if (c >= 'A') {
            result = (char) (c - 'A' + 'a');
        } else {
            result = c;
        }
        return result;
    }
}
